You only need to match the tile you have with one of the 2 ends already on the board.\r\n\r\nPlaying Dominos game requires, if you want to win most times, of course, a lot of skill and some good luck. So, go ahead and have lots of fun playing this unique game. Your goal is to achieve a certain score to win the game.\r\nIn order to get the pieces (or tiles, or bones) together, the number of pips at the end of each of the tiles must match. It is that simple. Go ahead, look no further. Start playing the best domino game right now. YOU will LOVE it.\r\n\r\n- Block dominoes: basically the same as Draw Dominoes. The main difference is you have to pass your turn if you run out of options (whereas you can pick an extra domino from the boneyard in the previous mode).\r\n\r\n- Dominoes All Five: slightly more complex. Each turn, you need to add all ends of the board, and count the number of pips on them. If it is a multiple of five, you score those points. A bit difficult at first but you will quickly get it!\r\n\r\nBeautiful, simple, relaxing, easy to learn yet complex if you get to learn all the tricks!
